		    <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
        // Auto-scroll for desktop ticker (smooth automatic scrolling)
        function autoScrollDesktopTicker() {
            var $ticker = $('.ticker-container');
            if ($ticker.length === 0) return;
            
            var scrollAmount = $ticker.find('.news-item').first().outerWidth(true) + 15;
            var totalItems = $ticker.find('.news-item').length;
            var visibleItems = 3;
            
            if (totalItems > visibleItems) {
                $ticker.animate({scrollLeft: scrollAmount}, 400, function() {
                    var firstItem = $ticker.find('.news-item').first();
                    $ticker.append(firstItem.clone());
                    firstItem.remove();
                    $ticker.scrollLeft(0);
                    setTimeout(autoScrollDesktopTicker, 4000);
                });
            }
        }
        
        // Start auto-scroll if desktop ticker exists
        if ($('.ticker-container').length) {
            setTimeout(autoScrollDesktopTicker, 4000);
        }
        
        // Add home icon to first menu item if not present
        $('.nav-menu li:first-child a').each(function() {
            if (!$(this).find('i').length) {
                $(this).prepend('<i class="fas fa-home"></i>');
            }
        });
        
        // Enhanced sub-menu hover effects
        $('.nav-menu li').hover(
            function() {
                $(this).addClass('menu-hover');
                $(this).find('> a').css({
                    'background': '#1e88e5',
                    'color': 'white'
                });
            },
            function() {
                $(this).removeClass('menu-hover');
                $(this).find('> a').css({
                    'background': 'transparent',
                    'color': '#2c3e50'
                });
                // Reset first menu item color
                if ($(this).is(':first-child')) {
                    $(this).find('> a').css('color', '#0d6efd');
                }
            }
        );
    });
    </script>
